ü§ñ Telegram Mini App Contest

Prize fund: $50,000
Deadline: 23:59 on October 9th (Dubai time)
Who can participate: Everyone
Results: October 31st, 2023

Telegram is launching a contest for developers of Mini Apps like this one. One of the goals of this competition is to create a variety of examples and reusable tools for future Mini App developers.

The Task:

The task is to build any useful Mini App for Telegram and publish its client and server code on Github.

Your submission must include:
‚Ä¢ A GitHub repository containing the source code of your example Mini App, built from scratch. You can use any programming language for the server-side code. The source code of your app must be easy to understand and reusable for any developer starting to build Mini Apps for Telegram. For more, see the ‚ÄúMini App requirements‚Äù section below.
‚Ä¢ Comprehensive and organized documentation in English, including a setup guide. Ensure the guide addresses every element of your solution, and the documentation details all potential errors and exceptions. It should be written in a user-friendly way that is approachable even for inexperienced developers. Translations in other languages are welcome too.

---

Mini App requirements:
‚Ä¢ Design a simple yet functional app. For reference, see @DurgerKingBot or @wallet.
‚Ä¢ Your solution should include at least one fully functional Mini App example. Example apps are allowed to showcase fictional services or generate placeholder data, such as creating a mock store.
‚Ä¢ It is strictly prohibited to implement a browser view of actual webpages, the Mini App must be a separate entity built from scratch solely for its purpose. For example a "Weather App" submission that only provides a browser view for an existing weather website is not allowed. That said, actual webpages are allowed for authorization flows where a user is required to sign up or log in to use the service.
‚Ä¢ Recommended Mini App categories include games, dating, community management, venue booking, e-commerce, —Åontent editing, etc.
‚Ä¢ Each additional Mini App example can qualify for extra rewards, but only if it represents a different app category.

Evaluation Criteria:
We will evaluate each submission's code and documentation quality from the developer perspective, as well as its example Mini Apps from the user perspective. The app should be useful for developers, users, or both.
____

@ContestBot will begin accepting submissions at a later date. We will further clarify the submission instructions closer to the deadline.

GOSH Announcements 28.09.2023 18:14:48
In reply to this message
GOSH Launches Fast, Scalable, Free To Use Layer 2 For Ethereum

With 12 key Launch Partners presenting unique, innovative use cases

Today GOSH, a git on-chain DAO-platform, announced that it runs as Ethereum Layer 2.

GOSH is an advanced scalable asynchronous sharded blockchain that allows select partners to run smart contracts on-chain for Free, making GOSH the first and only Freemium Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain.

GOSH stores and processes git objects entirely on-chain, allowing for fully decentralized management of repositories through GOSH DAOs, which are made automatically when creating any decentralized repository. GOSH is a TVM-based blockchain using Asynchronous Solidity tailored for a sharded development environment on top of Ethereum, providing high speeds and great scalability. GOSH currently runs over 2,000 DAOs and over 56 million git object smart contracts have been deployed so far.

GOSH decentralization and security is guaranteed by Ethereum. In final production, all contract state transitions on GOSH L2 are verified by Ethereum, withdrawing funds from either blockchain is easy, and to break the system would require both Ethereum and GOSH to be corrupted or stopped simultaneously. GOSH is the only formally verified Git implementation. And because developing on GOSH means using smart contracts for every merge, commit, and pull request, GOSH is the first development platform where the more code you write the more secure it becomes.

GOSH L2 is launching with 12 Partners: GBA, Ethernity Cloud, DeVote, GEX, DeSci World, Q, deScier, WOW DAO, Pruvendo, Hero2Quest, Triscale, Viete.

GOSH is a production ready on-chain Git DAO platform that can be accessed here while GOSH L2 is a fully trustless solution, accessible with limited functionality as a Beta right within the GOSH user interface.

To try it now, go to: https://gosh.sh and create an account.

GOSH Announcements 28.09.2023 20:01:21

GOSH Partners With deScier To Become New Standard In Alternative Scientific Publishing

Building infrastructures for a new future for science on GOSH Layer 2

Today GOSH, a decentralized git on-chain DAO platform, announced a partnership with deScier, a researcher-led community that applies blockchain technology for science, with initiatives is to facilitate scientific collaboration through The DeSci Journal, a Decentralized Science Journal, to develop a new git standard for submission of research code and data within alternative scientific publications.

Nowadays, scientists have 0%, yes, zero percent, of their copyright from legacy publishing houses. Together these publishing houses generate as much revenue as the music industry, at about 26 billion US Dollars per annum. The DeSci Journal is a starting point for scholars to be in contact with a new form of publishing and financing for their scientific research.

deScier is based on a collaborative economy sharing earnings with Editors, Reviewers and other Members involved in the peer-reviewing and publication processes. GOSH‚Äôs role as git standard for the purpose of decentralized supplementary data storage in alternative publishing strengthens and cements the advancement of DeSci publications, and science more broadly.

GOSH‚Äôs version control system git on-chain allows for a seamless transition for scientists into a decentralized framework, permitting them to truly own their research.

As part of the partnership, GOSH will build a pipeline to allow editors and reviewers to coordinate working on scientific articles. GOSH as an operational layer in the peer-review process for deScier‚Äôs Journal will offer authors a platform to publish their peer-reviewed research while holding 100% of their copyright. This is the next step in GOSH‚Äôs long standing support for decentralized science through projects such as Jocelyn DAO.

Join deScier DAO on GOSH at https://app.gosh.sh/o/descier

GOSH Announcements 28.09.2023 21:21:19

GOSH Partners with DeVote to Provide Truly Anonymous Online Voting in Private and Public Elections and for DAOs on GOSH

Building tools to champion the democratic process, reflecting the needs of a new digital world


Today GOSH, a decentralized git on-chain DAO platform, announced its partnership with DeVote, a blockchain based remote voting technology pioneer, to integrate its zero knowledge proof, truly anonymous remote voting mechanism to be used by DAOs on GOSH. DeVote‚Äôs voting mechanism enables members of DAOs to remain anonymous when voting on repository decisions. And GOSH ‚Äî the most scalable blockchain platform with a Freemium business model ‚Äî allows DeVote to run any type of public or private elections 100% on-chain, at any scale.

GOSH offers select partners gas-free smart contract usage, opening the possibility to run large scale elections on-chain. DeVote is currently participating in the elections technology tender announced by a national elections committee of a 100 million voter country.

DeVote and GOSH both actively participate in Government Blockchain Association (GBA) efforts to connect private companies with government customers and bring to the forefront new solutions for critical public sector needs. The expansion of the use of truly anonymous voting in GOSH‚Äôs ecosystem is expected to play a critical role to encourage the adoption of zero knowledge technologies in public and private sectors around the world.

Both GOSH and DeVote are presenting the partnership at the UN‚Äôs Internet Governance Forum in Kyoto (LINK)

Links: https://www.devoteusa.com https://gosh.sh

GOSH Announcements 28.09.2023 22:13:00
In reply to this message
GOSH Partners With FLEX To Launch The GOSH Decentralized Exchange ‚Äî GEX


The first gas free, fastest, fully on-chain Decentralized Limit Order Book Exchange, on GOSH, Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain

Today GOSH, a decentralized git on-chain DAO platform, announced a partnership with FLEX, a decentralized and distributed limit order book exchange, to launch the GOSH Decentralized Exchange (GEX) on the GOSH Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain. GEX offers traders unmatched performance, a familiar user experience, censorship-resistance, and a full security guarantee that make it a truly decentralized alternative to match any centralized exchange in production today.

Features and benefits of GEX include:

Gas-free trades: GEX will run as a GOSH native application, thus requiring no gas fees. Like on centralized exchanges, GEX Commissions are paid in the native currency of the trading pair.

Censorship-resistance: GEX is a software bundle that can be installed locally on a user computer, so no web server is involved. The software bundle itself can be downloaded, or compiled from, the source code available on GOSH‚Äôs decentralized Git on-chain service.

Performance: GEX runs on GOSH‚Äôs sharded, multi-threaded blockchain. Each trading pair price point in GEX is a separate set of smart contracts making it capable of parallel processing of an unprecedented number of trades.

Guaranteed Security: GEX contracts are in the process of Formal Verification by Pruvendo, a member of GOSH DAO, providing the highest level of software security available. Formal verification is the definitive final stage of any software‚Äôs security, and today is used by the space, avionics, transportation, and atomic industries, and many others. Formally Verified GEX will be fully ready for institutional adoption of any size.

GEX User Experience: GEX‚Äôs user experience is following trading industry standards with interface closely resembling that of a regular centralized exchange.

Join GEX DAO to participate in GEX decentralized community

# ton-space-weaknes-poc.py
from cryptography.hazmat.backends import default_backend
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.ciphers import Cipher, algorithms, modes


key = open('key.bin', 'rb').read()
iv = open('iv.bin', 'rb').read()
shard1 = open('shard1.bin', 'rb').read()
ciphertext = shard1
# Initialize AES-GCM cipher
cipher = Cipher(
algorithms.AES(key),
modes.GCM(iv),
backend=default_backend()
)

# Decrypt without authentication tag
decryptor = cipher.decryptor()
plaintext = decryptor.update(ciphertext)

print(plaintext)

GOSH Announcements 29.09.2023 00:23:23
In reply to this message
DeSciWorld Partners With GOSH To Set New Digital Standard For DeSci Research

GOSH is fast becoming a new digital standard for decentralized science, so that scientists the world over can leverage decentralized repository governance tools to advance, and encourage deeper collaboration within, the decentralized science ecosystem. With the launch of GOSH L2 DeSci World has migrated its Awesome DeSci repository to become a DAO on GOSH

DeSciWorld and GOSH are co-organizing the DeSci.Israel conference, set between 24th of March and 6th of April 2024, with specific dates pending final confirmation. Universities and scientific associations across Europe, UK, USA, South America, Africa, as well as with other blockchain associations, DAOs, projects, and independent researchers are slated to appear. Topics will include:

Decentralized tools on-chain and new scientific standards for increasing overall research quality and reproducibility

DeSci opportunities for Scientists At Risk

DAO Governance in decentralized research groups

‚ÄúThis partnership between GOSH and DeSciWorld aims to expand and develop groundbreaking use cases within DeSci with the focus on improving accessibility to, and reproducibility of, scientific research, which for too long, has been gatekept,‚Äù said DeSciWorld Founder Joshua Bate. ‚ÄúTools such as GOSH allow scientists to fully exploit the possibilities of decentralized ownership and collaboration.‚Äù

Our partnership with DeSciWorld is an embodiment of mutual respect and shared goals. It‚Äôs a reflection of our joint commitment to furthering decentralization as standard for transparent, unrestricted science. This collaboration symbolizes the initial phase of an enduring partnership aimed at implementing more complex and innovative solutions, integrating decentralized ownership, token incentives, and governance over each repository.

The link to sign up for the conference: https://app.gosh.sh/o/desci-israel-2024

GOSH Announcements 29.09.2023 16:52:45
In reply to this message
GOSH partners with Q to offer a dispute resolution system to Decentralized Autonomous Organizations

Offering an immutable on-chain dispute resolution system to DAOs on GOSH


GOSH, a decentralized git on-chain DAO platform, announced a partnership with Q. The Q Protocol provides a universal layer for Governance Security in the decentralized world. One of the features of Q is an integrated dispute resolution process, which enables DAOs on GOSH to settle disputes in a fair and transparent way.

DAOs on GOSH can now write up a constitution of their own, laying down the community‚Äôs rules. If decisions are suspected to be unconstitutional, they can be challenged via Q‚Äôs dispute resolution framework. This ensures that conflicts are resolved and the DAO community‚Äôs values are upheld.

Q is a completely new governance framework, building on and going beyond code is law. It enables discretionary decisions, democratizes access to international private law, and ensures a fair resolution of disputes on GOSH, and the decentralized world more broadly.

GOSH offers developers and organizations a decentralized governance model on-chain. Every repository is a community-run DAO with no single owner. Q‚Äôs decentralized governance system for the Web3 world allows DAOs on GOSH to work through legal frameworks and even binding contracts based on international private law. Decentralized protocols are a viable alternative to old-world legal systems, courts, and institutions.

GOSH now runs as Ethereum Layer 2. An advanced, scalable, asynchronous sharded blockchain that allows select partners to run smart contracts on-chain for Free, GOSH is the fastest, most scalable, and the first and only Freemium Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain. And because GOSH L2 supports any asset ERC-20 Tokenization with a click of a button, GOSH offers easy ecosystem integration for any project. This allows Q‚Äôs dispute resolution system to extend to any DAO on different networks seamlessly.

More about GOSH
More about Q

GOSH Partners With Triscale To Shape the Future of Environmental Credits

GOSH, now Ethereum Layer 2, and Triscale, a leading provider of infrastructural solutions for planetary challenges, have teamed up to reshape environmental credit accessibility via blockchain technology. This collaboration embodies Triscale and GOSH‚Äôs collective commitment to championing technology for addressing planetary challenges. The partnership concentrates on pioneering the advancement of environmental credits and empowering bilateral trade agreements between countries to curb the rise of greenhouse gas emissions.

We believe in technology‚Äôs indispensable role in achieving Sustainable Development Goals, and the aim is for Triscale and GOSH to create an ecosystem where even the smallest players in the environmental credits market can generate revenue, without being pushed out by larger entities.

This partnership signifies a mutual vision to leverage technology for addressing planetary challenges, offering efficient solutions and aligning economic frameworks for a sustainable future.

Triscale facilitates a capture-and-secure system for ESG & Impact project originators, providing easy oversight, reporting, and data insights, all while ensuring the creation of top-quality, measurable products. This collaboration promises more impact per dollar for philanthropy, higher ROI for investors, enhanced performance, and productivity for all actors and managers, and unparalleled transparency and accountability for governments and regulators.

For more about Triscale visit website

GOSH Announcements 30.09.2023 23:27:40
In reply to this message
GOSH Announces Integration With Pruvendo To Provide Automated Formal Verification Capabilities to Users

GOSH, a decentralized git on-chain freemium DAO platform and Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain, today announced its integration with Pruvendo, a software security firm specializing in formal verification, with a strategic target to offer developers on GOSH formal verification capabilities to guarantee the security of their code. The partnership aims to optimize development and maintenance costs, improve software quality, and provide unprecedented levels of code security through formal verification.

This integration with Pruvendo, running on both TVM and EVM, will be able to detect the ‚Äò.sol‚Äô extension in repository files, highlight essential elements of the file to allow developers to write specific verification statements on each markdown element, which can offer an automatic proof of the solidity code‚Äôs correctness.

Pruvendo offers a state-of-the-art SaaS for graphical specification creation, coupled with a formal verification engine, ensuring code conforms to the formulated specification. This interface empowers software engineers to interact with familiar tools seamlessly, thus allowing engineers without advanced mathematical proficiency to utilize the tool effectively.

GOSH is an advanced asynchronous sharded blockchain that allows select partners to run smart contracts on-chain for Free, making GOSH the fastest, most scalable, and the first and only Freemium Ethereum Layer 2 blockchain.

To get more information join Pruvendo‚Äôs DAO on GOSH

GOSH announces that the Artificial Intelligence & Secure Software Supply Chain Working Groups run by the Government Blockchain Association will operate as DAOs on GOSH, facilitating decentralized decision making and collaborative work on group documents and source code. As part of its ongoing activities to apply blockchain solutions by connecting governments to private entities around the world, GBA is hosting the Blockchain Assurance & Standardization Dynamic Coalition (BAS-DC) at the United Nations Internet Governance Forum (IGF). The centerpiece of the DC-BAS is the Blockchain Maturity Model (BMM), a framework to evaluate the trustworthiness of blockchain solutions, and the Artificial Intelligence and Secure Software Supply Chain Groups are part of UN Dynamic Coalition.

The partnership moves forward discourse on blockchain-based security for AI and software supply chains üöÄ

This year‚Äôs Internet Governance Forum (IGF) annual conference is held in Kyoto, Japan, hosted by the government of Japan, under the general theme: ‚ÄúInternet We Want - Empowering All People.‚Äù The meeting will feature approximately 300 sessions organized by many different stakeholders to discuss a variety of Internet issues
